Benchmarks

Benchmark Evidence, Not a Leaderboard

The website renders committed static artifacts. Benchmark timing is interpreted beside the generated current-support matrix instead of restating support posture here.

Current support source

Benchmarks reuse the status matrix.

Runtime support counts come from docs/status/runs-today-support-matrix.json. The benchmark artifact supplies timing and coverage context; it is not the source of truth for support claims.

33support rows
18executable
5feature-gated
5claim/platform blocked

Support claim boundary: current-state discoverability only; this matrix does not expand runtime support or authorize production, package, performance, object-store, lakehouse, Foundry, REST, or Spark-replacement claims.

Public front doors

Route rows name the user-facing prepared paths.

The benchmark bundle publishes route-identity rows for the high-level Python front doors. These rows are not timing rows; they bind the public surface to the route lane, preparation boundary, reuse manifest, and no-fallback posture.

Front door not_timing_row_route_identity_only

ShardLoom Prepare-Once First Query

ctx.prepare_vortex('fact.csv', workspace='target/shardloom-prepared').query('selective filter').collect()

Route timing dashboard

Route lanes are the comparison surface.

Stage pieces explain a ShardLoom route; they are not competing product lanes. Warm prepared and native Vortex rows stay labeled by start state.

Stage attribution

ShardLoom stage pieces explain route cost.

Preparation, query, output, evidence, and diagnostic context are separated from route-level comparisons so a warm prepared slice cannot be read as a cold end-to-end route. The next promoted artifact should show CSV/JSONL text-adapter RecordBatch import and writer-byte Vortex digest evidence before any new performance claim is made.

RouteRowsSource admissionSource readParse/decodeSource -> Vortex arrayVortex writeVortex reopen/verifyPrepared lookup/createVortex scanOperator computeResult sinkEvidence renderTotal route

Schema: shardloom.website.route_runtime_status.v1. Boundary: stage attribution explains why a ShardLoom route took time; stage pieces are not competing product lanes.

Runtime fast path

Runtime timing is separate from output and evidence rendering.

Sub-ms prepared/native query work can coexist with larger sink or evidence-render costs because route timing, output delivery, evidence capture, and certificate linkage are reported as separate buckets.

Artifact table: Runtime Fast Path Versus Evidence Path.

RouteRowsRuntime executionOutput deliveryEvidence captureEvidence renderCertificate linkEvidence render route totalCertificate status
ShardLoom Prepare-Once First Query1200.44 ms2.76 ms0.00 ms3.69 ms0.00 ms0/120 excluded from route totallinked_certified_runtime_execution: 120

ShardLoom Native Vortex Query1200.38 ms2.53 ms0.00 ms3.14 ms0.00 ms0/120 excluded from route totallinked_certified_runtime_execution: 120

Schema: shardloom.route_fast_path_attribution.v1. Boundary: runtime execution timing, output delivery, evidence capture, evidence render, and certificate linking are separate interpretation buckets; fast-path timing is not a performance superiority claim.

Operator mode inventory

Runtime support is not encoded-native support.

Rows can be scoped-runtime-supported while their operators remain residual-native or materialized-temporary. Encoded-native execution is a separate claim with its own blocker code and promotion candidate.

Prepare-once reuse

Amortization is shown as route math.

The prepared route keeps first-query cost visible, then shows how the same preparation cost amortizes across repeated prepared executions.

Benchmark constitution

Rows need route, correctness, environment, and no-fallback proof before claims.

The manifest names the row validator and the field set required before any benchmark row can become claim-grade. Current static artifacts remain interpretation evidence, not public performance claims.

Schema
shardloom.benchmark_constitution_validation.v1
Validator
scripts/check_benchmark_constitution.py
Claim gate
not_claim_grade
Performance claim allowed
false

Required row fields: benchmark_result_row, route_identity, route_runtime_status, dataset_source_admission, preparation_route, execution_route, output_route, claim_readiness_boundary, correctness_proof, hardware_profile, build_profile, cold_warm_state, stage_timings, route_timing_ledger, cold_lane_attribution, cost_unit_fields, no_fallback_proof, external_baseline_boundary.

Cold-lane attribution

Cold ingest bottlenecks stay attached to the route.

The promoter classifies each row before publication and labels the dominant cold-stage bottleneck. Missing stage splits block claim-grade interpretation instead of letting cold preparation or harness overhead hide inside a single timing number.

Runtime status

Runtime support is separate from claim readiness.

A row can be scoped-runtime-supported without authorizing performance, production, or Spark-replacement claims. External unsupported rows are baseline limitations, not ShardLoom runtime gaps.

ScopeRowsInterpretation
ShardLoom unsupported rows0ShardLoom runtime gaps in the promoted comparative roster
External baseline unsupported rows6External engine limitation rows; not ShardLoom runtime gaps
route_runtime_status=external_baseline_only720published row status vocabulary
route_runtime_status=scoped_runtime_supported600published row status vocabulary

Status vocabulary: external_baseline_only, feature_gated, fixture_smoke_only, scoped_runtime_supported, unsupported.

Claim-gate distribution

Evidence quality is not the same as runtime support.

Timing rows remain local context, not superiority proof. Compatibility cold timing is not pure query speed. Runtime support, evidence quality, and claim authorization are shown as separate layers.

Claim-grade closeout

ShardLoom gaps and external baseline limits are counted separately.

This page keeps runtime status, evidence quality, and claim authorization separate. External baseline unsupported rows do not imply a ShardLoom route gap.

ScopeCurrent rowsTargetPlan item

External baseline rowsexternal_baseline_only rows remain comparison contextvisible baseline-only rows; never fallback executionGAR-BENCH-PUB-1 / GAR-RUNTIME-IMPL-5J
